<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кирка.html>кирка</a> (13374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. Possibly, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">κερκίς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kerkís</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">küräk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кирка.html>кирка́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kirká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кирка.html>кирки́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кирка.html>ки́рки</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кирка.html>кирки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кирка.html>ки́рок</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кирко́вый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pickaxe</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">киркомоты́га</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kirkomotýga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кирка́-моты́га</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kirká-motýga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kirche</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:церковь.html>це́рковь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cerkovʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кирпич.html>кирпич</a> (2941)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Turkic language">Old Turkic</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="otk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kerpič</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">adobe, brick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">кірпіш</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kirpiş</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kerpiç</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">кирбес</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kirbes</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">kərpic</i>, etc.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>ки́са</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kísa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>ки́сы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>ки́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>кис</a></b>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kese</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">kisə</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>киса́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kisá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>кисы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>кисы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>кис</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> purse, moneybag, drawstring bag

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кисель.html>кисе́ль</a> (11517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kyselь</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кисель.html>кисе́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kisélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кисель.html>киселя́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кисель.html>кисели́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кисель.html>киселе́й</a></b>)

<ol><li>kisel, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kissel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:kissel">kissel</a> (a <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> jellied dessert made by cooking berry juice or other fruit juice with milk, flour and oatmeal, thickened with starch)</li>

***кисло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́сло</a> (15960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kíslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́сло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kíslo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ки́сло" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кисле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ки́сло" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кисле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dispiritedly, in a dejected manner</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in a sour or displeased manner</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kíslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***кислород.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислород.html>кислоро́д</a> (5401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kíslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-род</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-rod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give birth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">oxygène</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kíslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ота́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-otá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислота.html>кислота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kislotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислота.html>кислоты́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислота.html>кисло́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислота.html>кисло́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>acid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молочный.html>моло́чная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислота.html>кислота́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">molóčnaja <b>kislotá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">lactic acid</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***кислый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a> (5597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kys(ь)lъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kíslyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кисле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кисле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sour
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kísloje</b> jábloko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sour apple</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kísloje</b> molokó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sour milk</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fermented, sour
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>те́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kísloje</b> tésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sourdough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капуста.html>капу́ста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kíslaja</b> kapústa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sauerkraut</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kíslyje</b> šči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sauerkraut soup</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">sour soup</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dispirited, disheartened, crestfallen, down in the dumps
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> како́й-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ty kakój-to <b>kíslyj</b> sevódnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you seem to be in low spirits today</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">imétʹ <b>kíslyj</b> vid</i> ― <span class="e-translation">look miserable</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to have a dispirited look</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> displeased, dissatisfied
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kíslaja</b> ulýbka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sour/half-hearted smile</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кислый.html>ки́слое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdélatʹ <b>kísloje</b> licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pull/make a wry face</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***киснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:киснуть.html>ки́снуть</a> (27620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киса.html>кис</a>(лый)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kis(lyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киснуть.html>ки́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kísnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокиснуть.html>проки́снуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скиснуть.html>ски́снуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn sour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel depressed, to mope <i>(around)</i>, to languish</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вскиса́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vskisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***кисточка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кисточка.html>ки́сточка</a> (11957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кисть.html>кисть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kistʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-очка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-očka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кит.html>кит</a> (6967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">китъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kitŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κῆτος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kêtos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кит.html>кит</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kit</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кит.html>кита́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кит.html>киты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кит.html>кито́в</a></b>)

***китель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>ки́тель</a> (6770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kittel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>ки́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>ки́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>ки́тели</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>кители́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>ки́телей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китель.html>кителе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>type of a military uniform</li></ol>

***кичиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кичиться.html>кичи́ться</a> (25080)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кычити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kyčiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кычити ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kyčiti sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kyčiti</i>, derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kyka</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кичиться.html>кичи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kičítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put on airs; to boast, to brag</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кичли́вый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kičlívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***кишеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишеть.html>кише́ть</a> (10970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кишеть.html>кише́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kišétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to infest, to overrun</li>
<li>to swarm, to pullulate</li>
<li>to be infested</li>
<li>to abound, to be abundant</li>
<li>to crawl with</li></ol>

***кишка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a> (4179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kyšьka</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kišká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишки́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишо́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gut, intestine, bowel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tónkaja kišká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">small intestine</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>то́лстая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tólstaja kišká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">large intestine</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">двенадцатипе́рстная <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvenadcatipérstnaja kišká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">duodenum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>пряма́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prjamája kišká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rectum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слепой.html>слепа́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slepája kišká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blind gut, caecum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишка́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>тонка́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó kišká tonká!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he isn't up to it!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> giblets, pluck</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> insides, contents, spares</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hose (for watering)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tunnel, tunnel-like room</li></ol>
